to the terms of his 2016 restricted stock unit (&#8220;RSU&#8221;) and stock option awards.&#160; These waivers will permit Mr. Bensen, upon retirement, to vest in all outstanding RSU awards, subject to the original performance-based vesting conditions, and to continue to vest in his outstanding stock options pursuant to the original vesting schedule, which shall remain outstanding until the original expiration date.&#160; In addition, the Committee provided Mr. Bensen service credit through March 1, 2017 in order to enable him to vest in full in his 2016 stock option award (as opposed to 75%).&#160; In exchange, Mr. Bensen has agreed to an extension of his non-compete period following his retirement, from the Company&#8217;s customary eighteen month period to twenty-four months.</font></div><div><br></div><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr
